Let me tell you a story... 

 

My story.... 

 

I am Aaliyah Mae Ramosa.. 17 years old na ako ngayon.. but this story is wayback my high school life.. 
When I fell in love with a guy who doesn't seem to care...It started with a simple joke.. pero ako, nahulog 
sa kanya.. And that hurts a lot.. kasi he didn't catch me.. ;( 

 

*Characters*

Chapter 1: Sophomore's Crush 

 

I can't believe that time flies faster.. Grabe, 2nd year high school na ako.. New friends, new life, new 
acquaintances... 

 

Papasok na ako sa school, first day ngayon, kaya for sure, puro introduction of teachers and classmates

sections namin. Tsk.. Sana naman mga close ko mga classmates ko pa rin ngayon..

It had been very hard for me, for us to accept what the doctor said. 

 

"Her brain was damaged by the accident. May amnesia siya. Retrograde amnesia. Which means, 
she can't reacall some memories and people of the past. It's beyond ordinary forgetfulness." 

 

She doesn't even know her name. 

 

Kasalanan ko 'to! 

 

Ayokong umiyak. Ayokong makita siyang nahihirapan. 

 

Nakalabas na siya ng ospital pero parang wala pa rin. 

 

I'm here in their house in Antipolo. 

 

Naririnig ko, masaya yung boses niya from her room. 

 

Hindi naman nagalit sakin ang parents niya. 

 

Yun nga lang, this is going to be the last time na makikita ko siya. 

 

Her Dad said it wouldn't be good for Aaliyah if I continued seeing her. 

 

"Hi Paul! Tara na?!" ^___________^ 

"Tara. ^__^" 

 

Pupunta kami ngayon sa school. Sa garden. 

 

"Saan ba talaga tayo pupunta? Sabi ni Mama, may sasabihin ka daw sakin?" 

 

Nginitian ko lang siya. 

 

Ang lungkot isipin na ganito siya. 

 

Maayos kami. 

 

Pero bakit kailangan mangyari pa ang ganito? 

 

"Nandito na tayo." 


"Dito ba ang school natin?" 

 

I nodded. 

 

"Tara dun sa garden. ^__^" 

"Malaki rin pala ang school natin no?" 

"Ano palang gagawin natin sa graden?" 

"May.. May sasabihin lang ako sa'yo. ^_^" 

 

Hinawakan ko ang kamay niya. 

 

Ang lambot. 

 

Katulad pa rin ng dati. 

 

Ang mahirap lang, hindi niya alam kung anong nararamdaman niya sa akin. 

 

Hindi niya alam kung sino ako sa buhay niya. 

 

Pinaupo ko siya sa isa sa mga benches doon. 

 

"Aaliyah, ako nga pala si Paul. Paul Justine De Luna." 

 

Iniabot ko ang kamay ko sa kanya and she took it. 

 

We shook hands. She looks happy. 

 

"Una sa lahat, ako nga pala yung lagi mong kaaway dito. Ako yung HATEST guy mo dito sa 
school. Hanggang sa mag-third year tayo, nagbago yung lahat. Natuto kasi akong magmahal e. 
Lumambot yung puso ko sa'yo. Hindi na kita inasar simula noon. Simula noon, nagbago lahat. 
Nalaman ko, mahal mo pala ako. Nung una, napag-tripan pa kita about dun. Pero all of a sudden, I 
fell in love with you. I felt something strange about you. Yun pala yung feeling na never kong 
naramdman. Yung feeling na, mahal na pala kita." 

 

"Boyfriend ba kita?" 

 

"No. Hindi Aaliyah. Hindi tayo. Hindi naging tayo." 

 

"Pero mahal kita tapos mahal mo ako diba? Bakit hindi tayo?" 

 

"Maraming nangyari. Maraming bagay ang hindi mo na dapat malaman pa. I just want to let you 
know that I'm the reason kung bakit ka nagkaganyan. Kasalanan ko ang lahat. Kaya ka 
naaksidente ay dahil sa akin. Ako ang may kasalanan. Ako! Kaya dapat magalit ka sakin! Dapat 
hindi mo ako kinakaibigan!" 

 

"Teka.. Wag kang umiyak." 

 

"Sorry Aaliyah. I'm sorry for all the pains. Sorry for giving you this kind of life. You don't deserve 
this. Mas mabuti pa siguro kung ako na lang yung nagkaganyan." 

 

"Pero, wala naman na tayong magagawa. Please stop crying. T__T Naiiyak din ako. Wag kang ganyan." 

 

Once again, kinuha ko yung kamay niya. 

 

"Ano to?" 

 


"That's a keychain. Itago mo. Please, ingatan mo." 

 

"Okay. Ano 'to? HAYILAA? ^__^ Friends tayo ha?" 

 

Pinunasan ko na yung luha ko. I grabbed her hands. 

 

I knelt in front of her. 

 

"Aaliyah, I want you to know. You're the very first and last girl I would love. Keep it in your mind. 
I'll just be around. No matter what happens, kung ano man ang malaman mo, sana.. sana... 
MAHALIN MO PA RIN AKO." 

 

I kissed her hand. 

 

"Tara na, ihahatid na kita sa inyo. ^_^" 

 

"Okay." 

 

------------------------------------------------- 

 

WEEKS AFTER.. 

 

I wish I were a robot so that I won't feel this kind of pains. 

 

I'm totally wounded by my own mistake. 

 

She has all the spaces in my heart.. 

 

And I know, no one can ever fill that place. 

 

No one else can ever take that place. 

 

I never wanted to say goodbye... 

 

I need to be strong.. 

 

The only way I could let her go... 

 

In this case, 

 

She can't remember anything, 

 

She wouldn't be hurt so bad if I leave.. 

 

I know we're hopeless. 

 

Our love is hopeless. 

 

We can never be together. 

 

We weren't MEANT TO BE. 

 

TIME can heal all the anguish of the wound, but the LOSS cannot be REPAIRED. 

 

It's as simple as.. I WILL STILL LOVE HER EVEN WE'RE FAR.. 

 


BUT I KNOW... 

 

DEEP INSIDE ME... 

 

IT'S GOING TO BE A LIFE LIKE HELL. 

 

I never had her. 

 

And I guess.. 

 

IT'S NEVER DESTINED TO HAPPEN. 

 

This story closes... 

 

In two words with LOVE. 

 

This maybe painful.. 

 

This maybe goodbye.. 

 

But there will be another HELLO. 

 

In this HOPELESS LOVE. 

 

*END*
